### Test 11 — PASS

**Question**: how many games did the San Francisco Giants play the Los Angeles Dodgers in 2025

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT COUNT(*) AS game_count FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE ((t_home.name = 'San Francisco Giants' AND t_away.name = 'Los Angeles Dodgers') OR (t_home.name = 'Los Angeles Dodgers' AND t_away.name = 'San Francisco Giants')) AND YEAR(g.game_date) = 2025 AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final';
```

**Rows**: 1

**Timing**: LLM=0.178s | DB=0.128s | Total=0.306s
**Source**: example

---

### Test 12 — PASS

**Question**: game_pk, winner, game date how many games did the San Francisco Giants play the Los Angeles Dodgers in 2025

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (100) g.game_pk, CASE WHEN g.teams__home__score > g.teams__away__score THEN t_home.name ELSE t_away.name END AS winner, g.game_date FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE ((t_home.name = 'San Francisco Giants' AND t_away.name = 'Los Angeles Dodgers') OR (t_home.name = 'Los Angeles Dodgers' AND t_away.name = 'San Francisco Giants')) AND YEAR(g.game_date) = 2025 AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final' ORDER BY g.game_date;
```

**Rows**: 14

**Timing**: LLM=0.212s | DB=0.421s | Total=0.632s
**Source**: example

---

### Test 13 — PASS

**Question**: game_pk, winner or loser, game date for all double headers in the National League in 2025

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (100) g.game_pk, t_home.name AS home_team_name, t_away.name AS away_team_name, g.teams__home__score, g.teams__away__score, CASE WHEN g.teams__home__score > g.teams__away__score THEN t_home.name WHEN g.teams__away__score > g.teams__home__score THEN t_away.name ELSE 'Tie' END AS winner, CASE WHEN g.teams__home__score < g.teams__away__score THEN t_home.name WHEN g.teams__away__score < g.teams__home__score THEN t_away.name ELSE 'Tie' END AS loser, g.game_date, g.double_header FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE YEAR(g.game_date) = 2025 AND g.double_header = 'Y' AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND (t_home.league__name = 'National League' OR t_away.league__name = 'National League') ORDER BY g.game_date, g.game_pk;
```

**Rows**: 4

**Timing**: LLM=0.17s | DB=0.211s | Total=0.381s
**Source**: example

---

### Test 14 — PASS

**Question**: game_pk, opponent, winner or loser, score and game date how many regular season games did the San Francisco Giants play National League West opponents in 2025 and what were the results

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (100) g.game_pk, t_home.name AS home_team, t_away.name AS away_team, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'San Francisco Giants' THEN 'Home' ELSE 'Away' END AS giants_home_or_away, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'San Francisco Giants' AND g.teams__home__score > g.teams__away__score THEN 'Winner' WHEN t_home.name = 'San Francisco Giants' AND g.teams__home__score < g.teams__away__score THEN 'Loser' WHEN t_away.name = 'San Francisco Giants' AND g.teams__away__score > g.teams__home__score THEN 'Winner' WHEN t_away.name = 'San Francisco Giants' AND g.teams__away__score < g.teams__home__score THEN 'Loser' ELSE 'Tie' END AS giants_result, g.teams__home__score AS home_score, g.teams__away__score AS away_score, g.game_date FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE YEAR(g.game_date) = 2025 AND g.series_description = 'Regular Season' AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND (t_home.name = 'San Francisco Giants' OR t_away.name = 'San Francisco Giants') AND t_home.division__name = 'National League West' AND t_away.division__name = 'National League West' ORDER BY g.game_date;
```

**Rows**: 52

**Timing**: LLM=0.321s | DB=0.313s | Total=0.634s
**Source**: example

**SQL**: MATCH


### Test 18 — PASS

**Question**: player, position, signing bonus for the TOP 3 signing bonus for each round in 2025 draft

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT d.pick_round AS round, d.person__full_name, d.person__primary_position__name, CAST(d.signing_bonus AS decimal(18,2)) AS signing_bonus FROM (SELECT *, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY pick_round ORDER BY CAST(ISNULL(NULLIF(signing_bonus, ''), '0') AS decimal(18,2)) DESC) AS rn FROM dw.draft WHERE year = 2025 AND signing_bonus IS NOT NULL AND signing_bonus <> '') d WHERE d.rn <= 3 ORDER BY d.pick_round, CAST(d.signing_bonus AS decimal(18,2)) DESC;
```

**Rows**: 75

**Timing**: LLM=0.146s | DB=0.141s | Total=0.288s
**Source**: example

### Test 19 — PASS

**Question**: year, round, position, pick count for each draft round in 2020-2025

**SQL**: MATCH


### Test 22 — PASS

**Question**: pitcher, pitcher hand, batter side, pitch type, for strikeout pitches total strikeouts called or swinging and total strikeouts over 20

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT pitcher_name, pitcher_hand, batter_side, pitch_type, total_strikeouts, called_k, swinging_k FROM (SELECT p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type, COUNT(*) AS total_strikeouts, SUM(CASE WHEN p.is_called_strike = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS called_k, SUM(CASE WHEN p.is_whiff = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS swinging_k, AVG(p.start_speed) AS avg_velo, AVG(p.spin_rate) AS avg_spin, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn FROM dw.pitch_core p WHERE p.strikes = 2 AND (p.is_called_strike = 1 OR p.is_whiff = 1) AND p.season = 2025 GROUP BY p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type HAVING COUNT(*) > 20) ranked WHERE rn = 1 ORDER BY pitcher_name, batter_side;
```

**Rows**: 491

**Timing**: LLM=0.59s | DB=1.954s | Total=2.544s
**Source**: example

---

### Test 23 — PASS

**Question**: pitcher, pitcher hand, batter side, pitch type, for first pitches

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT pitcher_name, pitcher_hand, batter_side, pitch_type FROM (SELECT p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type, COUNT(*) AS total_strikeouts, SUM(CASE WHEN p.is_called_strike = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS called_k, SUM(CASE WHEN p.is_whiff = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS swinging_k, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn FROM dw.pitch_core p WHERE p.pitch_number = 1 AND (p.is_called_strike = 1 OR p.is_whiff = 1) AND p.season = 2025 GROUP BY p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type HAVING COUNT(*) > 20) ranked WHERE rn = 1 ORDER BY pitcher_name, batter_side;
```

**Rows**: 696

**Timing**: LLM=0.339s | DB=1.899s | Total=2.239s
**Source**: example

### Test 24 — PASS

**Question**: pitcher name, season, pitch type, total pitch, usage, average velocity, average spin rate, whiff rate, in play rate and strike rate for Top 20 pitchers based on strike rate

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (20) full_name, season, pitch_description, total_pitches, usage_pct, avg_velocity, avg_spin_rate, whiff_rate, in_play_rate, strike_rate FROM (SELECT p.full_name, f.season, t.pitch_description, f.total_pitches, f.usage_pct, f.avg_velocity, f.avg_spin_rate, f.whiff_rate, f.in_play_rate, f.strike_rate, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY f.pitcher_id, f.season ORDER BY f.total_pitches DESC) AS rn FROM dw.pitcher_pitch_type_features f JOIN dw.pitch_type t ON t.pitch_type = f.pitch_type LEFT JOIN dw.mlbplayers p ON p.id = f.pitcher_id WHERE f.pitch_type IS NOT NULL AND p.full_name IS NOT NULL AND f.total_pitches > 200 AND f.season = 2025) ranked WHERE rn <= 3 ORDER BY strike_rate DESC;
```

**Rows**: 20

**Timing**: LLM=0.229s | DB=0.137s | Total=0.366s
**Source**: example

### Test 34 — PASS

**Question**: average exit velocity and barrel rate by season 2020 to 2025

**SQL**: MATCH



### Test 99 — PASS

**Question**: how many shutouts did each team pitch in 2025 regular season

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT shutout_team, COUNT(*) AS shutouts FROM (SELECT CASE WHEN teams__home__score = 0 THEN teams__away__team__name WHEN teams__away__score = 0 THEN teams__home__team__name END AS shutout_team FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2025' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND (teams__home__score = 0 OR teams__away__score = 0) AND is_tie = 0) s WHERE shutout_team IS NOT NULL GROUP BY shutout_team ORDER BY shutouts DESC;
```

### Test 100 — PASS

**Question**: home wins and away wins for each team in 2025 regular season

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT team, SUM(home_win) AS home_wins, SUM(away_win) AS away_wins FROM (SELECT teams__home__team__name AS team, 1 AS home_win, 0 AS away_win FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2025' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND teams__home__is_winner = 1 UNION ALL SELECT teams__away__team__name AS team, 0 AS home_win, 1 AS away_win FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2025' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND teams__away__is_winner = 1) w GROUP BY team ORDER BY home_wins DESC;
```

### Test 113 — PASS

**Question**: largest margin of victory games in 2025 regular season top 10

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (10) game_pk, teams__home__team__name AS home_team, teams__away__team__name AS away_team, teams__home__score AS home_score, teams__away__score AS away_score, ABS(teams__home__score - teams__away__score) AS run_margin, CASE WHEN teams__home__score > teams__away__score THEN teams__home__team__name ELSE teams__away__team__name END AS winning_team, game_date FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2025' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final' ORDER BY run_margin DESC;
```

### Test 114 — PASS

**Question**: win loss record for each team in 2025 regular season

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT team, SUM(wins) AS wins, SUM(losses) AS losses, CAST(SUM(wins) AS float) / NULLIF(SUM(wins) + SUM(losses), 0) AS win_pct FROM (SELECT teams__home__team__name AS team, CASE WHEN teams__home__is_winner = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS wins, CASE WHEN teams__home__is_winner = 0 AND is_tie = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS losses FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2025' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final' UNION ALL SELECT teams__away__team__name AS team, CASE WHEN teams__away__is_winner = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS wins, CASE WHEN teams__away__is_winner = 0 AND is_tie = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS losses FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2025' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final') r GROUP BY team ORDER BY win_pct DESC;
```

**Rows**: 30

**Timing**: LLM=0.271s | DB=0.35s | Total=0.622s
**Source**: example

### Test 145 — PASS

**Question**: players who have won awards with multiple different teams across their career

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT pt.player_name,COUNT(DISTINCT pt.team_id) AS teams_count,COUNT(a.player_name) AS total_awards,STRING_AGG(pt.name, ', ') AS teams FROM (SELECT DISTINCT a.player_name,a.team_id,t.name FROM dw.award_recipients a JOIN dw.teams t  ON t.id = a.team_id) pt JOIN dw.award_recipients a ON a.player_name = pt.player_name GROUP BY pt.player_name HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT pt.team_id) > 1 ORDER BY teams_count DESC, total_awards DESC;
```

**Rows**: 448

**Timing**: LLM=0.126s | DB=2.263s | Total=2.389s
**Source**: example

### Test 179 — PASS

**Question**: active players drafted in the same year as their MLB debut year

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (100) p.full_name, p.draft_year, p.mlb_debut_date, p.primary_position__name, p.birth_city, p.birth_country FROM dw.mlbplayers p WHERE p.active = 1 AND p.draft_year IS NOT NULL AND p.mlb_debut_date IS NOT NULL AND CAST(p.draft_year AS nvarchar) = LEFT(p.mlb_debut_date, 4) ORDER BY p.draft_year DESC, p.full_name;
```

**Rows**: 3

### Test 199 — PASS

**Question**: how many games did the New York Yankees play the Boston Red Sox in 2025

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT COUNT(*) AS game_count FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE ((t_home.name = 'New York Yankees' AND t_away.name = 'Boston Red Sox') OR (t_home.name = 'Boston Red Sox' AND t_away.name = 'New York Yankees')) AND YEAR(g.game_date) = 2025 AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final';
```

**Rows**: 1

**Timing**: LLM=0.309s | DB=0.25s | Total=0.559s
**Source**: example

### Test 200 — PASS

**Question**: game_pk winner and date for all games between the Chicago Cubs and St. Louis Cardinals in 2025

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (100) g.game_pk, CASE WHEN g.teams__home__score > g.teams__away__score THEN t_home.name ELSE t_away.name END AS winner, g.game_date FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE ((t_home.name = 'Chicago Cubs' AND t_away.name = 'St. Louis Cardinals') OR (t_home.name = 'St. Louis Cardinals' AND t_away.name = 'Chicago Cubs')) AND YEAR(g.game_date) = 2025 AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final' ORDER BY g.game_date;
```

**Rows**: 13

**Timing**: LLM=0.763s | DB=0.353s | Total=1.116s
**Source**: example

### Test 201 — PASS

**Question**: all 2025 regular season games for the Los Angeles Dodgers including opponent score and result

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (162) g.game_pk, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'Los Angeles Dodgers' THEN 'Home' ELSE 'Away' END AS home_away, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'Los Angeles Dodgers' THEN t_away.name ELSE t_home.name END AS opponent, g.teams__home__score AS home_score, g.teams__away__score AS away_score, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'Los Angeles Dodgers' AND g.teams__home__is_winner = 1 THEN 'W' WHEN t_away.name = 'Los Angeles Dodgers' AND g.teams__away__is_winner = 1 THEN 'W' WHEN g.is_tie = 1 THEN 'T' ELSE 'L' END AS result, g.game_date FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE YEAR(g.game_date) = 2025 AND g.series_description = 'Regular Season' AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND (t_home.name = 'Los Angeles Dodgers' OR t_away.name = 'Los Angeles Dodgers') ORDER BY g.game_date;
```

**Rows**: 162

**Timing**: LLM=0.425s | DB=0.661s | Total=1.086s
**Source**: example

### Test 207 — PASS

**Question**: win loss record for each American League team in 2025 regular season

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT team, SUM(wins) AS wins, SUM(losses) AS losses, CAST(SUM(wins) AS float) / NULLIF(SUM(wins) + SUM(losses), 0) AS win_pct FROM (SELECT t_home.name AS team, CASE WHEN g.teams__home__is_winner = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS wins, CASE WHEN g.teams__home__is_winner = 0 AND g.is_tie = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS losses FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id WHERE g.season = '2025' AND g.series_description = 'Regular Season' AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND t_home.league__name = 'American League' UNION ALL SELECT t_away.name AS team, CASE WHEN g.teams__away__is_winner = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS wins, CASE WHEN g.teams__away__is_winner = 0 AND g.is_tie = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS losses FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE g.season = '2025' AND g.series_description = 'Regular Season' AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND t_away.league__name = 'American League') r GROUP BY team ORDER BY win_pct DESC;
```

**Rows**: 15

**Timing**: LLM=0.125s | DB=0.461s | Total=0.587s
**Source**: example

---

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (100) ps.season, ps.player__full_name, ps.team__name, ps.stat__games_played, ps.stat__at_bats, ps.stat__hits, ps.stat__home_runs, ps.stat__rbi, ps.stat__avg, ps.stat__obp, ps.stat__slg, ps.stat__ops FROM dw.player_stats ps WHERE ps.player__full_name = 'Ronald Acuna Jr.' ORDER BY ps.season DESC;
```

### Test 231 — PASS

**Question**: league pitching stats averages ERA WHIP and strikeouts in 2025

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT ps.league__name, ps.season, AVG(CAST(ps.stat__era AS decimal(10,2))) AS league_era, AVG(CAST(ps.stat__whip AS decimal(10,3))) AS league_whip, SUM(ps.stat__strike_outs) AS total_strikeouts FROM dw.player_stats ps WHERE ps.season = 2025 AND ps.stat__era IS NOT NULL AND ps.stat__games_started >= 5 AND ps.position__type = 'Pitcher' GROUP BY ps.league__name, ps.season ORDER BY ps.league__name;
```

**Rows**: 2

**Timing**: LLM=0.123s | DB=0.041s | Total=0.164s
**Source**: example

**SQL**: MATCH


### Test 274 — PASS

**Question**: average height and weight of active players by birth country

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT p.birth_country, COUNT(*) AS player_count, AVG(CAST(p.weight AS float)) AS avg_weight FROM dw.mlbplayers p WHERE p.active = 1 AND p.weight IS NOT NULL AND p.birth_country IS NOT NULL GROUP BY p.birth_country HAVING COUNT(*) >= 5 ORDER BY avg_weight DESC;
```

**Rows**: 13

**Timing**: LLM=0.144s | DB=0.048s | Total=0.193s

### Test 281 — PASS

**Question**: pitcher batter side and pitch type for most used pitches on three ball counts in 2025

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT pitcher_name, pitcher_hand, batter_side, pitch_type FROM (SELECT p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type, COUNT(*) AS total_pitches, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY p.pitcher_name, p.batter_side ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn FROM dw.pitch_core p WHERE p.balls = 3 AND p.season = 2025 GROUP BY p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type HAVING COUNT(*) > 20) ranked WHERE rn = 1 ORDER BY pitcher_name, batter_side;
```

**Rows**: 795

**Timing**: LLM=0.151s | DB=0.383s | Total=0.534s
**Source**: example

---

### Test 282 — PASS

**Question**: pitcher batter side and pitch type for pitches thrown with two strikes two balls in 2025

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT pitcher_name, pitcher_hand, batter_side, pitch_type FROM (SELECT p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type, COUNT(*) AS total_pitches, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY p.pitcher_name, p.batter_side ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn FROM dw.pitch_core p WHERE p.balls = 2 AND p.strikes = 2 AND p.season = 2025 GROUP BY p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type HAVING COUNT(*) > 20) ranked WHERE rn = 1 ORDER BY pitcher_name, batter_side;
```

**Rows**: 676

**Timing**: LLM=0.152s | DB=0.418s | Total=0.571s
**Source**: example

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (100) d.year, d.person__full_name, d.pick_number, d.person__primary_position__name, d.school__name, d.home__state FROM dw.draft d JOIN dw.school_type_lookup sl ON sl.school_name = d.school__name WHERE sl.school_type = 'Junior College' AND d.year = 2022 ORDER BY d.pick_number;
```

**Rows**: 16

**Timing**: LLM=0.128s | DB=0.213s | Total=0.34s
**Source**: example

### Test 317 — PASS

**Question**: name and position of first round picks in 2020 draft with name position and school

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (100) d.person__full_name, d.person__primary_position__name, d.school__name, d.home__state, CAST(ISNULL(NULLIF(d.signing_bonus, ''), '0') AS decimal(18,2)) AS signing_bonus FROM dw.draft d WHERE d.year = 2020 AND d.pick_round = '1' ORDER BY TRY_CAST(d.pick_number AS int);
```

**Rows**: 29

**Timing**: LLM=0.132s | DB=0.13s | Total=0.263s
**Source**: example

### Test 329 — PASS

**Question**: how many games did the New York Yankees play the Boston Red Sox in 2023

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT COUNT(*) AS game_count FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE ((t_home.name = 'New York Yankees' AND t_away.name = 'Boston Red Sox') OR (t_home.name = 'Boston Red Sox' AND t_away.name = 'New York Yankees')) AND YEAR(g.game_date) = 2023 AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final';
```

**Rows**: 1

**Timing**: LLM=0.167s | DB=0.34s | Total=0.508s
**Source**: example

---

### Test 335 — PASS

**Question**: game_pk winner and date for all games between the New York Mets and Philadelphia Phillies in 2025

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (100) g.game_pk, CASE WHEN g.teams__home__score > g.teams__away__score THEN t_home.name ELSE t_away.name END AS winner, g.game_date FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE ((t_home.name = 'New York Mets' AND t_away.name = 'Philadelphia Phillies') OR (t_home.name = 'Philadelphia Phillies' AND t_away.name = 'New York Mets')) AND YEAR(g.game_date) = 2025 AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final' ORDER BY g.game_date;
```

**Rows**: 13

**Timing**: LLM=0.179s | DB=0.359s | Total=0.539s
**Source**: example

---

### Test 339 — PASS

**Question**: all 2025 regular season games for the New York Mets including opponent score and result

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (162) g.game_pk, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'New York Mets' THEN 'Home' ELSE 'Away' END AS home_away, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'New York Mets' THEN t_away.name ELSE t_home.name END AS opponent, g.teams__home__score AS home_score, g.teams__away__score AS away_score, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'New York Mets' AND g.teams__home__is_winner = 1 THEN 'W' WHEN t_away.name = 'New York Mets' AND g.teams__away__is_winner = 1 THEN 'W' WHEN g.is_tie = 1 THEN 'T' ELSE 'L' END AS result, g.game_date FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE YEAR(g.game_date) = 2025 AND g.series_description = 'Regular Season' AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND (t_home.name = 'New York Mets' OR t_away.name = 'New York Mets') ORDER BY g.game_date;
```

**Rows**: 159

**Timing**: LLM=0.332s | DB=0.511s | Total=0.843s
**Source**: example

---

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (162) g.game_pk, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'Boston Red Sox' THEN 'Home' ELSE 'Away' END AS home_away, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'Boston Red Sox' THEN t_away.name ELSE t_home.name END AS opponent, g.teams__home__score AS home_score, g.teams__away__score AS away_score, CASE WHEN t_home.name = 'Boston Red Sox' AND g.teams__home__is_winner = 1 THEN 'W' WHEN t_away.name = 'Boston Red Sox' AND g.teams__away__is_winner = 1 THEN 'W' WHEN g.is_tie = 1 THEN 'T' ELSE 'L' END AS result, g.game_date FROM dw.games g JOIN dw.teams t_home ON g.teams__home__team__id = t_home.id JOIN dw.teams t_away ON g.teams__away__team__id = t_away.id WHERE YEAR(g.game_date) = 2024 AND g.series_description = 'Regular Season' AND g.status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND (t_home.name = 'Boston Red Sox' OR t_away.name = 'Boston Red Sox') ORDER BY g.game_date;
```

**Rows**: 162

**Timing**: LLM=0.163s | DB=0.279s | Total=0.443s
**Source**: example

### Test 360 — PASS

**Question**: shutout games in 2023 regular season with winning and losing team

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (100) game_pk, teams__home__team__name AS home_team, teams__away__team__name AS away_team, teams__home__score AS home_score, teams__away__score AS away_score, game_date, CASE WHEN teams__home__score > 0 AND teams__away__score = 0 THEN teams__home__team__name WHEN teams__away__score > 0 AND teams__home__score = 0 THEN teams__away__team__name END AS winning_team FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2023' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND (teams__home__score = 0 OR teams__away__score = 0) AND is_tie = 0 ORDER BY game_date;
```

---

### Test 362 — PASS

**Question**: win loss record for each team in 2023 regular season

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT team, SUM(wins) AS wins, SUM(losses) AS losses, CAST(SUM(wins) AS float) / NULLIF(SUM(wins) + SUM(losses), 0) AS win_pct FROM (SELECT teams__home__team__name AS team, CASE WHEN teams__home__is_winner = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS wins, CASE WHEN teams__home__is_winner = 0 AND is_tie = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS losses FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2023' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final' UNION ALL SELECT teams__away__team__name AS team, CASE WHEN teams__away__is_winner = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS wins, CASE WHEN teams__away__is_winner = 0 AND is_tie = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END AS losses FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2023' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final') r GROUP BY team ORDER BY win_pct DESC;
```

**Rows**: 30

**Timing**: LLM=0.135s | DB=0.244s | Total=0.38s
**Source**: example

---

### Test 363 — PASS

**Question**: games per month in 2023 regular season

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT MONTH(game_date) AS month_num, DATENAME(MONTH, game_date) AS month_name, COUNT(*) AS game_count FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2023' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final' GROUP BY MONTH(game_date), DATENAME(MONTH, game_date) ORDER BY month_num;
```

**Rows**: 8

**Timing**: LLM=0.072s | DB=0.22s | Total=0.293s
**Source**: example

### Test 364 — PASS

**Question**: home wins and away wins for each team in 2023 regular season

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT team, SUM(home_win) AS home_wins, SUM(away_win) AS away_wins FROM (SELECT teams__home__team__name AS team, 1 AS home_win, 0 AS away_win FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2023' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND teams__home__is_winner = 1 UNION ALL SELECT teams__away__team__name AS team, 0 AS home_win, 1 AS away_win FROM dw.games WHERE season = '2023' AND series_description = 'Regular Season' AND status__detailed_state = 'Final' AND teams__away__is_winner = 1) w GROUP BY team ORDER BY home_wins DESC;
```

**Rows**: 30

**Timing**: LLM=0.189s | DB=0.37s | Total=0.558s
**Source**: example

```sql
SELECT TOP (20) h.player_id, p.full_name, h.season, h.iso, h.slg, h.obp, h.plate_appearances FROM dw.hitter_season_features h LEFT JOIN dw.mlbplayers p ON p.id = h.player_id WHERE h.season = 2023 AND h.plate_appearances >= 100 ORDER BY h.iso DESC;
```

**Rows**: 20

**Timing**: LLM=0.103s | DB=0.039s | Total=0.142s

### Test 433 — PASS

**Question**: average exit velocity and barrel rate by season 2017 to 2025

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT h.season, COUNT(*) AS hitter_count, AVG(h.avg_exit_velocity) AS avg_exit_velo, AVG(h.barrel_rate) AS avg_barrel_rate, AVG(h.hard_hit_rate) AS avg_hard_hit_rate FROM dw.hitter_season_features h WHERE h.season BETWEEN 2017 AND 2025 AND h.plate_appearances >= 100 GROUP BY h.season ORDER BY h.season;
```

**Rows**: 6

**Timing**: LLM=0.171s | DB=0.058s | Total=0.23s
**Source**: example

### Test 441 — PASS

**Question**: pitcher name,season,pitch type,whiff rate,strike rate for top 20 pitchers based on whiff rate in 2024

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (20) full_name, season, pitch_description, total_pitches, usage_pct, avg_velocity, avg_spin_rate, whiff_rate, in_play_rate, strike_rate FROM (SELECT p.full_name, f.season, t.pitch_description, f.total_pitches, f.usage_pct, f.avg_velocity, f.avg_spin_rate, f.whiff_rate, f.in_play_rate, f.strike_rate, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY f.pitcher_id, f.season ORDER BY f.total_pitches DESC) AS rn FROM dw.pitcher_pitch_type_features f JOIN dw.pitch_type t ON t.pitch_type = f.pitch_type LEFT JOIN dw.mlbplayers p ON p.id = f.pitcher_id WHERE f.pitch_type IS NOT NULL AND p.full_name IS NOT NULL AND f.total_pitches > 200 AND f.season = 2024) ranked WHERE rn <= 3 ORDER BY whiff_rate DESC;
```

**Rows**: 20

**Timing**: LLM=0.245s | DB=0.059s | Total=0.305s
**Source**: example

---

### Test 442 — PASS

**Question**: pitcher name season pitch type for top 20 pitchers based on strike rate in 2024

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT TOP (20) full_name, season, pitch_description, total_pitches, usage_pct, avg_velocity, avg_spin_rate, whiff_rate, in_play_rate, strike_rate FROM (SELECT p.full_name, f.season, t.pitch_description, f.total_pitches, f.usage_pct, f.avg_velocity, f.avg_spin_rate, f.whiff_rate, f.in_play_rate, f.strike_rate, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY f.pitcher_id, f.season ORDER BY f.total_pitches DESC) AS rn FROM dw.pitcher_pitch_type_features f JOIN dw.pitch_type t ON t.pitch_type = f.pitch_type LEFT JOIN dw.mlbplayers p ON p.id = f.pitcher_id WHERE f.pitch_type IS NOT NULL AND p.full_name IS NOT NULL AND f.total_pitches > 200 AND f.season = 2024) ranked WHERE rn <= 3 ORDER BY strike_rate DESC;
```

**Rows**: 20

**Timing**: LLM=0.184s | DB=0.103s | Total=0.286s
**Source**: example

```sql
SELECT TOP (200) p.full_name, p.draft_year, p.primary_position__name, p.birth_state_province, p.birth_country, p.mlb_debut_date FROM dw.mlbplayers p WHERE p.active = 1 AND p.draft_year BETWEEN 2005 AND 2010 ORDER BY p.draft_year DESC, p.full_name;
```

### Test 525 — PASS

**Question**: pitcher batter side and pitch type for most used pitches on three ball counts in 2023

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT pitcher_name, pitcher_hand, batter_side, pitch_type FROM (SELECT p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type, COUNT(*) AS total_pitches, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY p.pitcher_name, p.batter_side ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn FROM dw.pitch_core p WHERE p.balls = 3 AND p.season = 2023 GROUP BY p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type HAVING COUNT(*) > 20) ranked WHERE rn = 1 ORDER BY pitcher_name, batter_side;
```

**Rows**: 816

**Timing**: LLM=0.138s | DB=0.415s | Total=0.554s
**Source**: example

### Test 529 — PASS

**Question**: pitcher pitcher hand batter side pitch type for strikeout pitches in 2023

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT pitcher_name, pitcher_hand, batter_side, pitch_type, total_strikeouts, called_k, swinging_k FROM (SELECT p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type, COUNT(*) AS total_strikeouts, SUM(CASE WHEN p.is_called_strike = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS called_k, SUM(CASE WHEN p.is_whiff = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS swinging_k, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn FROM dw.pitch_core p WHERE p.strikes = 2 AND (p.is_called_strike = 1 OR p.is_whiff = 1) AND p.season = 2023 GROUP BY p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type HAVING COUNT(*) > 20) ranked WHERE rn = 1 ORDER BY pitcher_name, batter_side;
```

**Rows**: 496

**Timing**: LLM=0.151s | DB=0.596s | Total=0.747s
**Source**: example

---

### Test 530 — PASS

**Question**: pitcher and batter side for first pitches total called strikes and whiffs in 2024

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql
SELECT pitcher_name, pitcher_hand, batter_side, pitch_type FROM (SELECT p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type, COUNT(*) AS total_pitches, SUM(CASE WHEN p.is_called_strike = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS called_k, SUM(CASE WHEN p.is_whiff = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS swinging_k, ROW_NUMBER() OVER (PARTITION BY p.pitcher_name, p.batter_side ORDER BY COUNT(*) DESC) AS rn FROM dw.pitch_core p WHERE p.pitch_number = 1 AND (p.is_called_strike = 1 OR p.is_whiff = 1) AND p.season = 2024 GROUP BY p.pitcher_name, p.pitcher_hand, p.batter_side, p.pitch_type HAVING COUNT(*) > 20) ranked WHERE rn = 1 ORDER BY pitcher_name, batter_side;
```

**Rows**: 696

**Timing**: LLM=0.165s | DB=0.534s | Total=0.699s
**Source**: example

**Question**: roster changes between 2024 and 2025 for the New York Mets players on 2025 but not 2024

**SQL**: MATCH

```sql

SELECT TOP (100) r.person__full_name, r.season, r.status__description FROM dw.rosters r JOIN dw.teams t ON t.id = r.parent_team_id WHERE t.name = 'Atlanta Braves' AND r.season = 2025 AND r.status__description IN ('Released', 'Waived', 'Traded') ORDER BY r.status__description, r.person__full_name;
```

**Rows**: 4

**Timing**: LLM=0.173s | DB=0.085s | Total=0.258s
**Source**: example
